			<div class="row">
				<div class="col-sm-7">
					<h1>Westminster Kennel Club</h1>
					<p>In 1877, New York was well on its way to becoming the world&#8217;s greatest city. This was the year that a group of sporting gentlemen decided that this would be a good time to hold a dog show in Manhattan. It didn&#8217;t take long before the Westminster Kennel Club, following the lead of its home town, would be on its way to becoming the world&#8217;s greatest dog show.</p>
					<a href="https://www.westminsterkennelclub.org/history/" class="about-link main-link">Our History</a>
